  <script>
   (function() {
		var a = document.querySelector('.h-nav-container');
		var b = a.querySelector('.h-nav-items');
		var c = a.querySelector('.h-nav-logo');
		var f = function () {
			var space = b.getBoundingClientRect().left - c.getBoundingClientRect().right;

			if (space > 40) {
				a.classList.remove('is-small');
				a.classList.add('is-big');
			} else {
				a.classList.remove('is-big');
				a.classList.add('is-small');
			}

			if (space > 300) {
				a.classList.add('is-huge');
			} else {
				a.classList.remove('is-huge');
			}
		};
		window.addEventListener('resize', f, false);
		f();
		window.dtResizeNav = f;
	}());
  </script>
  <div class="b-page" data-post-id="2634658" data-post-url="https://www.digitaltrends.com/gaming/loop-hero-explained/">
   <div class="b-page__wrapper">
    <section class="b-section h-section">
     <div class="b-page__inner">
      <div class="b-grid b-page__grid">
       <div class="b-post-tabbed-lists b-grid__post-tabbed-lists b-grid__cols4 b-grid__unlocked">
        <div class="b-synopsis-full b-synopsis-full--3-6 b-post-tabbed-lists__synopsis-full b-grid__cols3 b-grid__rows6">
         <div class="b-synopsis-full__meta">
          <div class="b-synopsis-full__alt-label">
           <a href="https://www.digitaltrends.com/computing/">
            Computing
           </a>
          </div>
          <h3 class="b-synopsis-full__title">
           <a class="b-synopsis-full__hot" href="https://www.digitaltrends.com/computing/apple-imac-pro-obituary-what-happened/" target="">
            From hero to zero: The stunning demise of the iMac Pro
           </a>
          </h3>
          <div class="b-synopsis-full__label">
           By
           <a class="author" href="https://www.digitaltrends.com/users/alexblake/">
            Alex Blake
           </a>
          </div>
